code: async def forward(self, taskInfo, extra_info):
    from collections import Counter
    
    # Initialize lists to keep track of sub-task outputs and agents
    sub_tasks = []
    agents = []
    
    # Sub-task 1: Summarize the plaintiff's claims and case details
    cot_instruction_1 = "Sub-task 1: Summarize the plaintiff's claims and case details based on the provided information."
    cot_agent_1 = LLMAgentBase(['thinking', 'answer'], 'Chain-of-Thought Agent', model=self.node_model, temperature=0.0)
    thinking1, answer1 = await cot_agent_1([taskInfo], extra_info, cot_instruction_1, is_sub_task=True)
    agents.append(f"CoT agent {cot_agent_1.id}, on the purpose of summarizing plaintiff claims, thinking: {thinking1.content}; answer: {answer1.content}")
    sub_tasks.append(f"Sub-task 1 output: thinking - {thinking1.content}; answer - {answer1.content}")
    
    # Sub-task 2: Summarize the defendant's defense and evidence
    cot_instruction_2 = "Sub-task 2: Based on the output of sub-task 1, summarize the defendant's defense and evidence."
    cot_agent_2 = LLMAgentBase(['thinking', 'answer'], 'Chain-of-Thought Agent', model=self.node_model, temperature=0.0)
    thinking2, answer2 = await cot_agent_2([taskInfo, thinking1, answer1], extra_info, cot_instruction_2, is_sub_task=True)
    agents.append(f"CoT agent {cot_agent_2.id}, on the purpose of summarizing defendant defense, thinking: {thinking2.content}; answer: {answer2.content}")
    sub_tasks.append(f"Sub-task 2 output: thinking - {thinking2.content}; answer - {answer2.content}")
    
    # New Sub-task 3a: Analyze the plaintiff's evidence and assess its credibility and relevance
    reflexion_instruction_3a = "Sub-task 3a: Based on the outputs of sub-task 1 and 2, analyze the plaintiff's evidence and assess its credibility and relevance."
    cot_agent_3a = LLMAgentBase(['thinking', 'answer'], 'Chain-of-Thought Agent', model=self.node_model, temperature=0.0)
    critic_agent_3a = LLMAgentBase(['feedback', 'correct'], 'Critic Agent', model=self.node_model, temperature=0.0)
    N_max_3a = self.max_round
    cot_inputs_3a = [taskInfo, thinking1, answer1, thinking2, answer2]
    thinking3a, answer3a = await cot_agent_3a(cot_inputs_3a, extra_info, reflexion_instruction_3a, 0, is_sub_task=True)
    agents.append(f"CoT agent {cot_agent_3a.id}, on the purpose of analyzing plaintiff's evidence, thinking: {thinking3a.content}; answer: {answer3a.content}")
    for i in range(N_max_3a):
        feedback3a, correct3a = await critic_agent_3a([taskInfo, thinking3a, answer3a], extra_info, reflexion_instruction_3a, i, is_sub_task=True)
        agents.append(f"Critic agent {critic_agent_3a.id}, on the purpose of feedback for plaintiff's evidence, thinking: {feedback3a.content}; answer: {correct3a.content}")
        if correct3a.content == 'True':
            break
        cot_inputs_3a.extend([thinking3a, answer3a, feedback3a])
        thinking3a, answer3a = await cot_agent_3a(cot_inputs_3a, extra_info, reflexion_instruction_3a, i + 1, is_sub_task=True)
        agents.append(f"CoT agent {cot_agent_3a.id}, on the purpose of refining plaintiff's evidence analysis, thinking: {thinking3a.content}; answer: {answer3a.content}")
    sub_tasks.append(f"Sub-task 3a output: thinking - {thinking3a.content}; answer - {answer3a.content}")

    # New Sub-task 3b: Analyze the defendant's evidence and assess its credibility and relevance
    reflexion_instruction_3b = "Sub-task 3b: Based on the outputs of sub-task 1 and 2, analyze the defendant's evidence and assess its credibility and relevance."
    cot_agent_3b = LLMAgentBase(['thinking', 'answer'], 'Chain-of-Thought Agent', model=self.node_model, temperature=0.0)
    critic_agent_3b = LLMAgentBase(['feedback', 'correct'], 'Critic Agent', model=self.node_model, temperature=0.0)
    N_max_3b = self.max_round
    cot_inputs_3b = [taskInfo, thinking1, answer1, thinking2, answer2]
    thinking3b, answer3b = await cot_agent_3b(cot_inputs_3b, extra_info, reflexion_instruction_3b, 0, is_sub_task=True)
    agents.append(f"CoT agent {cot_agent_3b.id}, on the purpose of analyzing defendant's evidence, thinking: {thinking3b.content}; answer: {answer3b.content}")
    for i in range(N_max_3b):
        feedback3b, correct3b = await critic_agent_3b([taskInfo, thinking3b, answer3b], extra_info, reflexion_instruction_3b, i, is_sub_task=True)
        agents.append(f"Critic agent {critic_agent_3b.id}, on the purpose of feedback for defendant's evidence, thinking: {feedback3b.content}; answer: {correct3b.content}")
        if correct3b.content == 'True':
            break
        cot_inputs_3b.extend([thinking3b, answer3b, feedback3b])
        thinking3b, answer3b = await cot_agent_3b(cot_inputs_3b, extra_info, reflexion_instruction_3b, i + 1, is_sub_task=True)
        agents.append(f"CoT agent {cot_agent_3b.id}, on the purpose of refining defendant's evidence analysis, thinking: {thinking3b.content}; answer: {answer3b.content}")
    sub_tasks.append(f"Sub-task 3b output: thinking - {thinking3b.content}; answer - {answer3b.content}")

    # New Sub-task 3c: Compare and contrast the evidence from both parties
    reflexion_instruction_3c = "Sub-task 3c: Based on the outputs of sub-task 3a and 3b, compare and contrast the evidence from both parties to identify key points of contention."
    cot_agent_3c = LLMAgentBase(['thinking', 'answer'], 'Chain-of-Thought Agent', model=self.node_model, temperature=0.0)
    critic_agent_3c = LLMAgentBase(['feedback', 'correct'], 'Critic Agent', model=self.node_model, temperature=0.0)
    N_max_3c = self.max_round
    cot_inputs_3c = [taskInfo, thinking3a, answer3a, thinking3b, answer3b]
    thinking3c, answer3c = await cot_agent_3c(cot_inputs_3c, extra_info, reflexion_instruction_3c, 0, is_sub_task=True)
    agents.append(f"CoT agent {cot_agent_3c.id}, on the purpose of comparing evidence, thinking: {thinking3c.content}; answer: {answer3c.content}")
    for i in range(N_max_3c):
        feedback3c, correct3c = await critic_agent_3c([taskInfo, thinking3c, answer3c], extra_info, reflexion_instruction_3c, i, is_sub_task=True)
        agents.append(f"Critic agent {critic_agent_3c.id}, on the purpose of feedback for evidence comparison, thinking: {feedback3c.content}; answer: {correct3c.content}")
        if correct3c.content == 'True':
            break
        cot_inputs_3c.extend([thinking3c, answer3c, feedback3c])
        thinking3c, answer3c = await cot_agent_3c(cot_inputs_3c, extra_info, reflexion_instruction_3c, i + 1, is_sub_task=True)
        agents.append(f"CoT agent {cot_agent_3c.id}, on the purpose of refining evidence comparison, thinking: {thinking3c.content}; answer: {answer3c.content}")
    sub_tasks.append(f"Sub-task 3c output: thinking - {thinking3c.content}; answer - {answer3c.content}")

    # New Sub-task 5a: Assess the possibility of reconciliation
    cot_sc_instruction_5a = "Sub-task 5a: Based on the outputs of sub-task 1, 2, 3a, 3b, and 3c, assess the possibility of reconciliation between the parties."
    N_5a = self.max_sc
    cot_agents_5a = [LLMAgentBase(['thinking', 'answer'], 'Chain-of-Thought Agent', model=self.node_model, temperature=0.5) for _ in range(N_5a)]
    thinking_mapping_5a = {}
    answer_mapping_5a = {}
    possible_answers_5a = []
    for i in range(N_5a):
        thinking5a, answer5a = await cot_agents_5a[i]([taskInfo, thinking1, answer1, thinking2, answer2, thinking3a, answer3a, thinking3b, answer3b, thinking3c, answer3c], extra_info, cot_sc_instruction_5a, is_sub_task=True)
        agents.append(f"CoT agent {cot_agents_5a[i].id}, on the purpose of assessing reconciliation, thinking: {thinking5a.content}; answer: {answer5a.content}")
        possible_answers_5a.append(answer5a.content)
        thinking_mapping_5a[answer5a.content] = thinking5a
        answer_mapping_5a[answer5a.content] = answer5a
    answer5a = Counter(possible_answers_5a).most_common(1)[0][0]
    thinking5a = thinking_mapping_5a[answer5a]
    answer5a = answer_mapping_5a[answer5a]
    sub_tasks.append(f"Sub-task 5a output: thinking - {thinking5a.content}; answer - {answer5a.content}")

    # New Sub-task 5b1a1: Identify specific financial documents needed to assess the vehicle loan
    cot_instruction_5b1a1 = "Sub-task 5b1a1: Based on the outputs of sub-task 1, 2, 3a, 3b, and 3c, identify specific financial documents needed to assess the vehicle loan."
    cot_agent_5b1a1 = LLMAgentBase(['thinking', 'answer'], 'Chain-of-Thought Agent', model=self.node_model, temperature=0.0)
    thinking5b1a1, answer5b1a1 = await cot_agent_5b1a1([taskInfo, thinking1, answer1, thinking2, answer2, thinking3a, answer3a, thinking3b, answer3b, thinking3c, answer3c], extra_info, cot_instruction_5b1a1, is_sub_task=True)
    agents.append(f"CoT agent {cot_agent_5b1a1.id}, on the purpose of identifying financial documents, thinking: {thinking5b1a1.content}; answer: {answer5b1a1.content}")
    sub_tasks.append(f"Sub-task 5b1a1 output: thinking - {thinking5b1a1.content}; answer - {answer5b1a1.content}")

    # New Sub-task 5b1a2: Request and obtain the identified financial documents from both parties
    reflexion_instruction_5b1a2 = "Sub-task 5b1a2: Based on the output of sub-task 5b1a1, request and obtain the identified financial documents from both parties."
    cot_agent_5b1a2 = LLMAgentBase(['thinking', 'answer'], 'Chain-of-Thought Agent', model=self.node_model, temperature=0.0)
    critic_agent_5b1a2 = LLMAgentBase(['feedback', 'correct'], 'Critic Agent', model=self.node_model, temperature=0.0)
    N_max_5b1a2 = self.max_round
    cot_inputs_5b1a2 = [taskInfo, thinking5b1a1, answer5b1a1]
    thinking5b1a2, answer5b1a2 = await cot_agent_5b1a2(cot_inputs_5b1a2, extra_info, reflexion_instruction_5b1a2, 0, is_sub_task=True)
    agents.append(f"CoT agent {cot_agent_5b1a2.id}, on the purpose of requesting financial documents, thinking: {thinking5b1a2.content}; answer: {answer5b1a2.content}")
    for i in range(N_max_5b1a2):
        feedback5b1a2, correct5b1a2 = await critic_agent_5b1a2([taskInfo, thinking5b1a2, answer5b1a2], extra_info, reflexion_instruction_5b1a2, i, is_sub_task=True)
        agents.append(f"Critic agent {critic_agent_5b1a2.id}, on the purpose of feedback for requesting financial documents, thinking: {feedback5b1a2.content}; answer: {correct5b1a2.content}")
        if correct5b1a2.content == 'True':
            break
        cot_inputs_5b1a2.extend([thinking5b1a2, answer5b1a2, feedback5b1a2])
        thinking5b1a2, answer5b1a2 = await cot_agent_5b1a2(cot_inputs_5b1a2, extra_info, reflexion_instruction_5b1a2, i + 1, is_sub_task=True)
        agents.append(f"CoT agent {cot_agent_5b1a2.id}, on the purpose of refining request for financial documents, thinking: {thinking5b1a2.content}; answer: {answer5b1a2.content}")
    sub_tasks.append(f"Sub-task 5b1a2 output: thinking - {thinking5b1a2.content}; answer - {answer5b1a2.content}")

    # New Sub-task 5b1b: Analyze the gathered financial records to determine responsibility
    cot_sc_instruction_5b1b = "Sub-task 5b1b: Based on the outputs of sub-task 5b1a2, analyze the gathered financial records to determine responsibility for the vehicle loan."
    N_5b1b = self.max_sc
    cot_agents_5b1b = [LLMAgentBase(['thinking', 'answer'], 'Chain-of-Thought Agent', model=self.node_model, temperature=0.5) for _ in range(N_5b1b)]
    thinking_mapping_5b1b = {}
    answer_mapping_5b1b = {}
    possible_answers_5b1b = []
    for i in range(N_5b1b):
        thinking5b1b, answer5b1b = await cot_agents_5b1b[i]([taskInfo, thinking5b1a2, answer5b1a2], extra_info, cot_sc_instruction_5b1b, is_sub_task=True)
        agents.append(f"CoT agent {cot_agents_5b1b[i].id}, on the purpose of analyzing financial responsibility, thinking: {thinking5b1b.content}; answer: {answer5b1b.content}")
        possible_answers_5b1b.append(answer5b1b.content)
        thinking_mapping_5b1b[answer5b1b.content] = thinking5b1b
        answer_mapping_5b1b[answer5b1b.content] = answer5b1b
    answer5b1b = Counter(possible_answers_5b1b).most_common(1)[0][0]
    thinking5b1b = thinking_mapping_5b1b[answer5b1b]
    answer5b1b = answer_mapping_5b1b[answer5b1b]
    sub_tasks.append(f"Sub-task 5b1b output: thinking - {thinking5b1b.content}; answer - {answer5b1b.content}")

    # New Sub-task 5b2: Evaluate the child custody arrangements
    reflexion_instruction_5b2 = "Sub-task 5b2: Based on the outputs of sub-task 1, 2, 3a, 3b, and 3c, evaluate the child custody arrangements based on legal standards and evidence."
    cot_agent_5b2 = LLMAgentBase(['thinking', 'answer'], 'Chain-of-Thought Agent', model=self.node_model, temperature=0.0)
    critic_agent_5b2 = LLMAgentBase(['feedback', 'correct'], 'Critic Agent', model=self.node_model, temperature=0.0)
    N_max_5b2 = self.max_round
    cot_inputs_5b2 = [taskInfo, thinking1, answer1, thinking2, answer2, thinking3a, answer3a, thinking3b, answer3b, thinking3c, answer3c]
    thinking5b2, answer5b2 = await cot_agent_5b2(cot_inputs_5b2, extra_info, reflexion_instruction_5b2, 0, is_sub_task=True)
    agents.append(f"CoT agent {cot_agent_5b2.id}, on the purpose of evaluating child custody arrangements, thinking: {thinking5b2.content}; answer: {answer5b2.content}")
    for i in range(N_max_5b2):
        feedback5b2, correct5b2 = await critic_agent_5b2([taskInfo, thinking5b2, answer5b2], extra_info, reflexion_instruction_5b2, i, is_sub_task=True)
        agents.append(f"Critic agent {critic_agent_5b2.id}, on the purpose of feedback for child custody arrangements, thinking: {feedback5b2.content}; answer: {correct5b2.content}")
        if correct5b2.content == 'True':
            break
        cot_inputs_5b2.extend([thinking5b2, answer5b2, feedback5b2])
        thinking5b2, answer5b2 = await cot_agent_5b2(cot_inputs_5b2, extra_info, reflexion_instruction_5b2, i + 1, is_sub_task=True)
        agents.append(f"CoT agent {cot_agent_5b2.id}, on the purpose of refining child custody arrangements, thinking: {thinking5b2.content}; answer: {answer5b2.content}")
    sub_tasks.append(f"Sub-task 5b2 output: thinking - {thinking5b2.content}; answer - {answer5b2.content}")

    # New Sub-task 5c: Synthesize the findings to make a comprehensive final judgment
    debate_instruction_5c = "Sub-task 5c: Based on the outputs of sub-task 5a, 5b1b, and 5b2, synthesize the findings to make a comprehensive final judgment. It is known that the following responses are not correct: 1. 判决准予原告朱某与被告党某1离婚，因双方婚姻关系已无法继续。 2. 婚生女党某2由原告朱某抚养，被告党某1每月支付抚养费1000元，直至孩子年满18周岁。 3. 被告党某1的孩子党佩妍由被告抚养。 4. 陕ＵＦ××××号车辆的剩余贷款由被告党某1承担。 5. 诉讼费由被告党某1承担. 6. 判决不准予原告朱某与被告党某1离婚，因证据不足以证明婚姻关系已无可挽回地破裂。婚生女党某2由原告朱某抚养，被告党某1每月支付抚养费1000元，直至孩子年满18周岁。被告党某1的孩子党佩妍由被告抚养。陕ＵＦ××××号车辆的剩余贷款由被告党某1承担。诉讼费由双方各自承担. 7. 判决准予原告朱某与被告党某1离婚，因双方婚姻关系已无法继续。婚生女党某2由原告朱某抚养，被告党某1每月支付抚养费1000元，直至孩子年满18周岁。被告党某1的孩子党佩妍由被告抚养。陕ＵＦ××××号车辆的剩余贷款责任难以明确分配，因双方对财务交易的主张缺乏具体证据支持，需提供进一步的财务文件和证据以作出明确判决。诉讼费由双方各自承担. 8. 判决准予原告朱某与被告党某1离婚，因双方婚姻关系已无法继续。婚生女党某2由原告朱某抚养，被告党某1每月支付抚养费1000元，直至孩子年满18周岁。被告党某1的孩子党佩妍由被告抚养。关于陕ＵＦ××××号车辆的剩余贷款责任，由于缺乏具体财务证据支持，暂无法做出明确判决，需提供进一步的财务文件和证据以作出明确判决。诉讼费由双方各自承担."
    max_round_5c = self.max_round
    debate_agents_5c = [LLMAgentBase(['thinking', 'answer'], 'Debate Agent', model=self.node_model, role=role, temperature=0.5) for role in self.debate_role]
    all_thinking_5c = [[] for _ in range(max_round_5c)]
    all_answer_5c = [[] for _ in range(max_round_5c)]
    for r in range(max_round_5c):
        for i in range(len(debate_agents_5c)):
            if r == 0:
                thinking5c, answer5c = await debate_agents_5c[i]([taskInfo, thinking5a, answer5a, thinking5b1b, answer5b1b, thinking5b2, answer5b2], extra_info, debate_instruction_5c, is_sub_task=True)
            else:
                input_infos_5c = [taskInfo, thinking5a, answer5a, thinking5b1b, answer5b1b, thinking5b2, answer5b2] + all_thinking_5c[r-1] + all_answer_5c[r-1]
                thinking5c, answer5c = await debate_agents_5c[i](input_infos_5c, extra_info, debate_instruction_5c, is_sub_task=True)
            agents.append(f"Debate agent {debate_agents_5c[i].id}, round {r}, on the purpose of making final judgment, thinking: {thinking5c.content}; answer: {answer5c.content}")
            all_thinking_5c[r].append(thinking5c)
            all_answer_5c[r].append(answer5c)
    final_decision_agent_5c = LLMAgentBase(['thinking', 'answer'], 'Final Decision Agent', model=self.node_model, temperature=0.0)
    thinking_final, answer_final = await final_decision_agent_5c([taskInfo, thinking5a, answer5a, thinking5b1b, answer5b1b, thinking5b2, answer5b2] + all_thinking_5c[-1] + all_answer_5c[-1], extra_info, debate_instruction_5c, is_sub_task=True)
    agents.append(f"Final Decision agent, on the purpose of final judgment, thinking: {thinking_final.content}; answer: {answer_final.content}")
    sub_tasks.append(f"Sub-task 5c output: thinking - {thinking_final.content}; answer - {answer_final.content}")

    final_answer = self.make_final_answer(thinking_final, answer_final, sub_tasks, agents)
    return final_answer
